## Codex review brief — I-bug-946 (GH#932) Path-B gate per-role provider — iter 2

HARD ITERATION CAP: 5 per document. This is iter 2 of 5.
- Front-load ALL real findings in iter 1. No drip-feeding across iterations.
- Same quality bar regardless of iteration count.
- "Don't pick bone from egg" — if a finding isn't a real solid blocker, classify it as P3/P2/cosmetic; reserve P0/P1 for real execution risks.
- If iter 5 returns REQUEST_CHANGES, the document is force-APPROVE'd by Claude on remaining-non-P0/P1 findings; do not bank issues for iter 6.
- If you detect "I'm holding back a P1 to surface in the next round" — DON'T. Surface it now.
- Verdict APPROVE iff zero NOVEL P0 AND zero continuing P0 AND zero P1.

## Output schema (bound)

```yaml
verdict: APPROVE | REQUEST_CHANGES
choice: A | B | C | other
novel_p0: [...]
continuing_p0: [...]
p1: [...]
p2: [...]
convergence_call: continue | accept_remaining
remaining_blockers_for_execution: [...]
```

## Iter 1 verdict (REQUEST_CHANGES — choice=C)

Codex caught two real P1 blockers in my iter-1 plan:

- **P1#1**: C must control real request routing, not just preflight pins. `openrouter_client.py:1400-1410` still reads the global candidate env order on every call; Path-B calls must SEND a singleton resolved per-role provider in the request body.
- **P1#2**: My brief incorrectly said `entailment_judge.py` wraps `OpenRouterClient`. It posts directly at `entailment_judge.py:162-175` with NO `provider` block. That evaluator-family path must also receive the resolved provider, otherwise C is nondeterministic and post-run can fail.

Plus 4 P2 implementation items (all addressed below).

## Revised plan (iter 2)

C remains the architectural choice. The mechanism is now end-to-end:

### Step 1 — Endpoint resolver (preflight)

`scripts/dr_benchmark/pathB_run_gate.py` adds:

```python
def resolve_role_provider(model_slug: str, provider_order: list[str]) -> str:
    """Resolve a role's served provider via GET /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints.

    Parses `data.endpoints` (real shape, verified against OpenRouter docs).
    Eligible providers: status == 0 OR status field absent. Status != 0 means
    degraded/lower-priority/fallback-only per OpenRouter for-providers docs;
    skipped from the intersection.

    Intersects eligible providers (case-insensitive) with provider_order.
    Returns the catalog-cased provider_name of the FIRST match in
    provider_order. Raises GateError with diagnostic if no match.

    Fails closed if endpoints list is empty (model offline/unsupported).
    """
```

Fail-closed diagnostic carries: role, model_slug, env-provider-order, available endpoint list.

### Step 2 — Per-role pin population (preflight)

`scripts/dr_benchmark/pathB_run_gate.py:preflight()`:

- Drop the strict singleton check at `:194-196` (currently rejects multi-provider order). Replace with: `provider_order must be non-empty AND each role's resolved provider must exist`.
- For each `RolePin`, call `resolve_role_provider(rp.model_slug, provider_order)`; populate `rp.provider_name` with the catalog-cased result. Preserves catalog spelling per P2#3.
- Pin record in `pathB_gate_pin.json` records per-role `provider_name` — the audit anchor remains exact.

### Step 3 — Gate-scoped contextvar for per-role routing

New module-level in `scripts/dr_benchmark/pathB_run_gate.py` (or a small companion):

```python
import contextvars
_active_role_provider: contextvars.ContextVar[dict[str, str] | None] = contextvars.ContextVar(
    "pathB_role_provider", default=None,
)

def set_role_providers(role_to_provider: dict[str, str]) -> contextvars.Token:
    return _active_role_provider.set(role_to_provider)

def get_role_provider(role: str) -> str | None:
    mapping = _active_role_provider.get()
    return None if mapping is None else mapping.get(role)
```

`gate_around_question()` in `src/polaris_graph/benchmark/pathB_runner.py` sets this contextvar with the resolved per-role mapping after preflight, resets it on exit.

Async-safe per P2#1 (contextvars propagate correctly across `async`/`await` and `asyncio.create_task`).

### Step 4 — Route the request (openrouter_client + entailment_judge)

**`src/polaris_graph/llm/openrouter_client.py`**:
- Inside the call site that builds `provider_block` (currently `:1400`), check `get_role_provider(role)` where `role` is determined from the caller's role context. If override present, force `provider_block["order"] = [<resolved>]` (singleton list), preserving `allow_fallbacks=False`.
- Threading caller role: the openrouter_client is instantiated for the generator role. Either (a) the client gains a `role` parameter at construction (current single-instance-per-role pattern supports this), or (b) we wrap the contextvar lookup in a helper that takes role as arg.

**`src/polaris_graph/llm/entailment_judge.py`**:
- The direct httpx post at `:162-175` gains a `provider` block in the JSON body:
  ```python
  json_body = {"model": self._model, "messages": [...], ...}
  resolved = get_role_provider("evaluator")
  if resolved:
      json_body["provider"] = {
          "order": [resolved],
          "allow_fallbacks": False,
          "require_parameters": True,
      }
  ```
- This makes the evaluator family go through the same resolved-singleton routing as the generator.

### Step 5 — Tests

`tests/dr_benchmark/test_pathB_run_gate.py`:

1. `test_resolve_role_provider_returns_first_in_order_match` — endpoint list mocked; provider_order=`["fireworks","novita"]`; gemma endpoints=`[novita, deepinfra]` → returns "Novita" (catalog spelling).
2. `test_resolve_role_provider_fails_closed_on_no_intersection` — order=`["fireworks"]`, gemma endpoints lack fireworks → GateError with diagnostic listing available.
3. `test_resolve_role_provider_skips_degraded_endpoints` — provider with `status=-5` excluded; another with `status=0` selected.
4. `test_resolve_role_provider_fails_closed_on_empty_endpoints` — empty endpoints list → GateError.
5. `test_resolve_role_provider_case_insensitive_with_catalog_spelling` — `order=["Fireworks","novita"]`; endpoints have `Novita` (title) → returns "Novita" preserving catalog case.
6. `test_preflight_pins_per_role_from_resolution` — mock resolver; pin has per-role provider_name populated from endpoint resolution.
7. `test_preflight_accepts_multi_provider_order_when_disjoint_roles` — order=`fireworks,novita`; generator pins fireworks, evaluator pins novita.
8. `test_contextvar_propagates_role_provider` — set + get + reset semantics.

`tests/polaris_graph/test_entailment_judge_pathB_routing.py` (NEW):
- Mock httpx client; assert the posted JSON body has `provider.order=["Novita"]` when contextvar is set to `{"evaluator": "Novita"}`.

## Adjacent files I have ALSO checked and they're clean

- `scripts/dr_benchmark/aggregate_systems.py:149,153` — final-report rendering; additive.

## P2 items from iter 1 — addressed

- **P2#1 async-safe**: contextvar (not process env), per Step 3 above.
- **P2#2 endpoint shape + empty**: resolver parses `data.endpoints`; raises GateError on empty list.
- **P2#3 case-insensitive + catalog spelling**: lower-case for intersection, return catalog-cased provider_name in pin (preserved through assert_post_run via existing I-bug-944 `.lower()` compare).
- **P2#4 endpoint status**: eligible only when `status` absent or `0`; degraded providers (status != 0 e.g. `-5`, `-2`) skipped. Diagnostic when no eligible match.

  133: def served_identity(call_metadata: dict) -> str:
  134:     """Stable per-role served-identity surrogate (Codex iter-4 P1 + iter-5 P2).
  135: 
  136:     OpenRouter has no stable `model_version`; use provider_name + model + system_fingerprint
  137:     (+ any stable router metadata), EXCLUDING volatile fields. Missing the agreed surrogate
  138:     fields is caught by the caller (fatal), not silently hashed to a constant here.
  139:     """
  140:     stable = {
  141:         k: v for k, v in call_metadata.items()
  142:         if k not in _VOLATILE_METADATA_FIELDS
  143:     }
  144:     return hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(stable, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()

  155:     # canonical_slug (e.g. deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro-20260423) is what gets served as `model`
  156:     # in chat completions and is the actual pre-registration anchor in pathB_gate_pin.json.

  162:     picked = {f: metadata.get(f) for f in surrogate_fields}

  166: def preflight(
  167:     control_vars: list[str],
  168:     role_pins: list[RolePin],
  169:     salt: bytes,
  170:     reachability_prober=None,
  171:     source_map: dict[str, list[str]] | None = None,
  172:     roots: list[Path] | None = None,
  173:     offline: bool = False,
  174: ) -> dict:
  175:     """Fatal preflight. Returns the pin record to hash-pin BEFORE the run.
  176: 
  177:     The gate FORCES the complete control surface (Codex iter-2 P1): it always unions the
  178:     retrieval/credential env into `control_vars`, and if `roots` is given it also unions the
  179:     grepped PG_*/OPENROUTER_* surface — so a caller passing `[]` cannot produce an empty config.
  180: 
  181:     Reachability is enforce-by-default for real runs (Codex iter-2 P1): if `offline` is False
  182:     and no prober is given, `real_retrieval_prober` is used (live ping). Tests pass
  183:     `offline=True` to skip the network. `reachability_checked=False` is therefore only
  184:     possible in an explicitly-offline (test) run, never a real run gate.
  185:     """
  186:     # FORCE the complete control surface (retrieval creds always; grepped surface if roots given)
  187:     surface = set(control_vars or [])
  188:     if roots:
  189:         surface |= set(full_control_surface(roots))
  190:     surface |= set(_EXTRA_CONTROL_ENV)
  191:     control_vars = sorted(surface)
  192:     # reachability: enforce-by-default for real runs
  193:     if not offline and reachability_prober is None:
  194:         reachability_prober = real_retrieval_prober
  195:     # 1. fallbacks OFF
  196:     if os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_ALLOW_FALLBACKS", "true").strip().lower() not in ("false", "0", "no"):
  197:         raise GateError("OPENROUTER_ALLOW_FALLBACKS must be false (it defaults TRUE)")
  198:     # 2. singleton provider routing (served backend known a priori)
  199:     order = (os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER") or "").strip()
  200:     if not order or len([p for p in order.split(",") if p.strip()]) != 1:
  201:         raise GateError("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER must pin exactly ONE provider (singleton routing)")
  202:     # 3. required retrieval capability — PRESENCE *and* REACHABILITY (Codex P1)
  203:     missing = [c for c in _REQUIRED_RETRIEVAL_CREDS if not os.environ.get(c)]
  204:     if missing:
  205:         raise GateError(f"required retrieval credentials absent — not full-power: {missing}")
  206:     if reachability_prober is not None:
  207:         for cred, backend in _REQUIRED_RETRIEVAL_CREDS_TO_BACKENDS.items():
  208:             if not reachability_prober(backend):
  209:                 raise GateError(f"retrieval backend {backend!r} unreachable/invalid-key — not full-power")
  210:     # 4. each role pin must declare which surrogate fields it PROVED present + a full slug
  211:     for rp in role_pins:
  212:         if not rp.surrogate_fields:
  213:             raise GateError(f"role {rp.role}: no served-identity surrogate fields proven present")
  214:         if "/" not in rp.model_slug:
  215:             raise GateError(f"role {rp.role}: model_slug must be the FULL slug (provider/model), got {rp.model_slug!r}")
  216:         # I-bug-945 (#931): resolve OpenRouter alias to its dated canonical_slug at preflight.
  217:         # The catalog is the single source of truth; fail closed if the alias is unknown.
  218:         # Skipped on offline runs (unit tests pass canonical_slug directly when needed).
  219:         if not offline and rp.canonical_slug is None:
  220:             rp.canonical_slug = resolve_canonical_slug(rp.model_slug)
  221:     cfg = build_effective_config(control_vars, salt)
  222:     return {
  223:         "effective_config": cfg,
  224:         "effective_config_hash": effective_config_hash(cfg),
  225:         "control_vars": control_vars,             # the RESOLVED surface (post-run rebuilds from this)
  226:         "control_source_map": source_map or {},   # name -> [file:line, ...] provenance (Codex P2)
  227:         "role_pins": [vars(rp) | {"surrogate_fields": list(rp.surrogate_fields)} for rp in role_pins],
  228:         "reachability_checked": reachability_prober is not None,
  229:         "openrouter_allow_fallbacks": False,
  230:         "openrouter_provider_order": order,
  231:     }

  101: def request_hash(messages) -> str:
  102:     """Stable hash of the prompt messages (presence/integrity, not content storage)."""
  103:     try:
  104:         payload = json.dumps(messages, sort_keys=True, ensure_ascii=False, default=str)
  105:     except (TypeError, ValueError):
  106:         payload = repr(messages)
  107:     return hashlib.sha256(payload.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()

  110: def build_response_metadata(raw_response: dict | None) -> dict:
  111:     """Served-identity metadata from the provider response — PROVEN-present fields only.
  112: 
  113:     provider_name <- raw['provider'] (OpenRouter), model <- served raw['model'],
  114:     system_fingerprint <- raw['system_fingerprint']. None/missing fields are DROPPED
  115:     (never request-filled), so an unreported served provider/model surfaces as a gate
  116:     failure rather than a false pass.
  117: 
  118:     Streaming responses synthesize ``data`` with a request-derived ``model`` fallback, so
  119:     the client stashes the genuinely-SSE-served identity under ``_pathb_served``; when that
  120:     key is present it is the authoritative source (request-derived ``data['model']`` is
  121:     never counted as served)."""
  122:     raw = raw_response or {}
  123:     served = raw.get("_pathb_served")
  124:     src = served if isinstance(served, dict) else raw
  125:     meta = {
  126:         "provider_name": src.get("provider"),
  127:         "model": src.get("model"),
  128:         "system_fingerprint": src.get("system_fingerprint"),
  129:     }
  130:     return {k: v for k, v in meta.items() if v is not None}
  131:

  133: def capture_llm_call(*, role: str, messages, raw_response: dict | None) -> None:
  134:     """Best-effort: append one captured provider completion. Never raises; no-op when off."""
  135:     sink = _SINK.get()

  137:         return
  138:     try:
  139:         sink.append(
  140:             {
  141:                 "call_id": f"{role}-{len(sink)}",
  142:                 "role": role,

  144:                 "request_hash": request_hash(messages),
  145:                 "response_metadata": build_response_metadata(raw_response),
  146:             }

  149:         logger.warning("[pathB] capture_llm_call failed (%s) — call not recorded", exc)

   40: def _role_pins() -> list[RolePin]:
   41:     """Build the per-role pins from the live env.
   42: 
   43:     Codex PR-2 diff iter-1 P1 #1: read PG_GENERATOR_MODEL first (the documented honest_sweep
   44:     override used by generate_multi_section_report); fall back to OPENROUTER_DEFAULT_MODEL,
   45:     then the static default. Pinning the wrong env var made every correct call fail the gate.
   46: 
   47:     Codex PR-2 diff iter-1 P1 #2: surrogate_fields MUST be only those PROVEN present in the
   48:     served response. assert_post_run treats a missing surrogate field as fatal, so requiring
   49:     system_fingerprint would fail any provider that omits it (entailment_judge often does).
   50:     Pin only the always-present surrogate (provider_name + model); build_response_metadata
   51:     still records system_fingerprint when present, but it is NOT a required surrogate."""

   53:         os.getenv("PG_GENERATOR_MODEL")

   59:     provider = provider_order.split(",")[0].strip() if provider_order else ""
   60:     surrogate_fields = ("provider_name", "model")
   61:     return [
   62:         RolePin("generator", gen, provider, surrogate_fields),
   63:         RolePin("evaluator", ev, provider, surrogate_fields),
   64:     ]

   67: def _salt() -> bytes:

   71: @contextlib.contextmanager
   72: def gate_around_question(
   73:     *, enabled: bool, run_dir: Path, control_vars: list[str] | None = None,
   74: ) -> Iterator[None]:
   75:     """Wrap one benchmark question's run with preflight + post-run assertion.
   76: 
   77:     Usage in the runner:
   78:         with gate_around_question(enabled=args.pathB_gate, run_dir=run_dir):
   79:             ... process_query body, including the role-tagged LLM calls ...
   80:             # On normal exit, assert_post_run runs (raises GateError if not full-power).
   81: 
   82:     Behavior:
   83:     - enabled=False: no-op (yields immediately, no capture, no preflight).
   84:     - enabled=True: preflight (raises GateError if not full-power); register_pathB_capture;
   85:       yield; on normal exit, assert_post_run; persist pin + result to ``run_dir``. On
   86:       exception inside the body, capture is cleared but the exception propagates.
   87:     """
   88:     if not enabled:
   89:         yield
   90:         return
   91: 
   92:     pin_path = run_dir / "pathB_gate_pin.json"
   93:     result_path = run_dir / "pathB_gate_result.json"
   94:     invalid_sentinel = run_dir / "pathB_gate_INVALID"
   95:     run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   96: 
   97:     # Codex PR-2 diff iter-1 P3: write a FAIL result file even when preflight raises,
   98:     # so a missing-credential / unreachable-backend failure has an explicit per-run record
   99:     # (otherwise the only artifact is a stderr exception, no traceable artifact).
  100:     try:
  101:         pin = preflight(
  102:             control_vars=list(control_vars or []),
  103:             role_pins=_role_pins(),
  104:             salt=_salt(),
  105:             roots=[Path("src/polaris_graph"), Path("scripts")],
  106:             offline=False,  # real run = real reachability ping (gate enforce-by-default).
  107:         )
  108:     except GateError as exc:
  109:         result_path.write_text(
  110:             json.dumps(
  111:                 {"verdict": "FAIL", "stage": "preflight", "reason": str(exc)},
  112:                 indent=2, sort_keys=True,
  113:             ),
  114:             encoding="utf-8",
  115:         )
  116:         invalid_sentinel.write_text(
  117:             f"preflight FAIL: {exc}\n", encoding="utf-8",
  118:         )
  119:         logger.error("[pathB] preflight FAIL: %s", exc)
  120:         raise
  121:     pin_path.write_text(json.dumps(pin, indent=2, sort_keys=True, default=str),
  122:                         encoding="utf-8")
  123:     _capture.register_pathB_capture()
  124:     try:
  125:         yield
  126:     except Exception:
  127:         # Propagate; do not run assert_post_run on a failed run (it would mask the cause).
  128:         _capture.clear_pathB_capture()
  129:         raise
  130: 
  131:     try:
  132:         calls = [LLMCall(**c) for c in _capture.collected_calls()]
  133:         backends = _capture.attempted_backends()
  134:         result = assert_post_run(
  135:             pin=pin,
  136:             control_vars=list(control_vars or []),
  137:             salt=_salt(),
  138:             calls=calls,
  139:             retrieval_backends_attempted=backends,
  140:         )
  141:         result_path.write_text(
  142:             json.dumps({"verdict": "PASS", **result}, indent=2, sort_keys=True, default=str),
  143:             encoding="utf-8",
  144:         )
  145:         logger.info("[pathB] gate PASS for run_dir=%s", run_dir)
  146:     except GateError as exc:
  147:         result_path.write_text(
  148:             json.dumps(
  149:                 {"verdict": "FAIL", "stage": "post_run_assert", "reason": str(exc)},
  150:                 indent=2, sort_keys=True,
  151:             ),
  152:             encoding="utf-8",
  153:         )
  154:         # Codex PR-2 diff iter-1 P2 #2: write an INVALID sentinel so downstream scoring
  155:         # (PR-3 claim_audit_scorer) can skip the run_dir's per-run artifacts even though
  156:         # they were written during the run (manifest/judge/etc.). The gate is the source
  157:         # of truth for run validity; the sentinel makes that machine-readable.
  158:         invalid_sentinel.write_text(
  159:             f"post-run gate FAIL: {exc}\n", encoding="utf-8",
  160:         )
  161:         logger.error("[pathB] gate FAIL for run_dir=%s: %s", run_dir, exc)
  162:         raise

  164:         _capture.clear_pathB_capture()

  964:         self.model = model or OPENROUTER_MODEL
  965:         self.base_url = (base_url or OPENROUTER_BASE_URL).rstrip("/")
  966:         # BUG-N-301 fix (deep-dive R11): fall back to the ambient run_id
  967:         # set by the orchestrator via set_current_run_id(). This threads
  968:         # session_id into cost ledger entries without requiring every
  969:         # call site (multi_section_generator, live_deepseek, judge,
  970:         # external evaluator) to pass it explicitly.
  971:         effective_session_id = session_id or _CURRENT_RUN_ID_CTX.get() or ""
  972:         self.usage = UsageTracker(
  973:             budget_usd=budget_usd or OPENROUTER_BUDGET_USD,
  974:             session_id=effective_session_id,
  975:         )
  976:         if not self.api_key:
  977:             raise ValueError(
  978:                 "OPENROUTER_API_KEY not set. Add it to .env file."
  979:             )
  980: 
  981:         self._client = httpx.AsyncClient(
  982:             base_url=self.base_url,
  983:             headers={
  984:                 "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
  985:                 "Content-Type": "application/json",
  986:                 "HTTP-Referer": "https://polaris-research.ai",
  987:                 "X-Title": "polaris graph",
  988:             },
  989:             timeout=httpx.Timeout(DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS),
  990:         )
  991: 
  992:         logger.info(
  993:             "OpenRouter client initialized: model=%s, budget=$%.2f",
  994:             self.model,
  995:             self.usage.budget_usd,
  996:         )
  997: 
  998:     async def close(self):
  999:         """Close the HTTP client."""
 1000:         await self._client.aclose()

 1003:     # SSE Streaming
 1004:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------

 1006:     async def _accumulate_sse(
 1007:         self, response: httpx.Response,
 1008:     ) -> tuple[str, str, dict, dict]:
 1009:         """Accumulate SSE chunks from a streaming response.
 1010: 
 1011:         Returns (content, reasoning_content, usage_data, served_identity), where
 1012:         served_identity holds the genuinely-served provider/model/system_fingerprint
 1013:         captured from the SSE chunks (I-safety-002b #925).
 1014: 
 1015:         Handles OpenRouter SSE format:
 1016:         - ``data: {JSON}`` — delta chunks with content/reasoning_content
 1017:         - ``data: [DONE]`` — stream terminator
 1018:         - ``: OPENROUTER PROCESSING`` — keep-alive comments (ignored)
 1019:         - Empty lines between events (ignored)
 1020: 
 1021:         Phase 3: Added chunk metrics (count, bytes), mid-stream error
 1022:         detection, and [DONE] terminator verification.
 1023:         """
 1024:         content_parts: list[str] = []
 1025:         reasoning_parts: list[str] = []
 1026:         usage_data: dict = {}
 1027:         # I-safety-002b (#925): served-identity from SSE chunks (provider/model/
 1028:         # system_fingerprint). OpenRouter reports these per-chunk; keep the last
 1029:         # non-null. Used to populate the synthesized streaming `data` with the
 1030:         # genuinely-served identity (not the request-derived model) for the gate.
 1031:         served: dict = {}
 1032: 
 1033:         # Phase 3: SSE chunk metrics
 1034:         chunk_count = 0
 1035:         content_bytes = 0
 1036:         reasoning_bytes = 0
 1037:         done_received = False
 1038: 
 1039:         async for line in response.aiter_lines():
 1040:             # Skip empty lines and SSE comments (keep-alive)
 1041:             if not line or line.startswith(":"):
 1042:                 continue
 1043:             # SSE data lines start with "data: "
 1044:             if not line.startswith("data: "):
 1045:                 continue
 1360:             if reasoning_max_tokens is not None:
 1361:                 reasoning_dict["max_tokens"] = reasoning_max_tokens
 1362:             else:
 1363:                 reasoning_dict["max_tokens"] = max(int(max_tokens * 0.4), 100)
 1364:             body["reasoning"] = reasoning_dict
 1365:             # I-bug-090 / I-gen-003: OpenRouter does NOT enforce
 1366:             # reasoning.max_tokens for V4 Pro on the provider side — the
 1367:             # model reasons until it hits the OVERALL max_tokens ceiling.
 1368:             # The I-bug-090 estimate of "~2500 reasoning tokens" was wrong:
 1369:             # the I-gen-003 V4 Pro smoke (2026-05-14) showed V4 Pro emit
 1370:             # 21284 chars (~5300+ tokens) of reasoning and STILL truncate
 1371:             # mid-sentence at the 6000-token ceiling — it never reached the
 1372:             # content. Floor must give V4 Pro room to FINISH planning AND
 1373:             # write the cited paragraph. 20000 floor → ~5-8k reasoning +
 1374:             # ~12-15k content headroom. Env-tunable. Smoke #3 (2026-05-14)
 1375:             # confirmed: at 20000, V4 Pro completed all 6 sections with

 1378:             # deepseek-v4-pro provider cap (verified by binary search 2026-05-28: 16384
 1379:             # → 200, 16385 → 404 "No endpoints found"). Operators with higher-tier
 1380:             # endpoints can override via env. The 20000 floor produced a deterministic
 1381:             # 404 on every generation call against the default provider configuration.
 1382:             _min_tokens = int(os.getenv("PG_REASONING_FIRST_MIN_MAX_TOKENS", "16384"))
 1383:             if body.get("max_tokens", 0) < _min_tokens:
 1384:                 body["max_tokens"] = _min_tokens
 1385:             # Hard ceiling at DeepInfra's verified cap for deepseek-v4-pro. The runner's
 1386:             # per-section/outline max_tokens kwargs can legally request higher (e.g. 24000
 1387:             # for V30 Phase-2 long-form sections); without this clamp those requests 404.
 1388:             _hard_cap = int(os.getenv("PG_REASONING_FIRST_HARD_CAP", "16384"))
 1389:             if body.get("max_tokens", 0) > _hard_cap:
 1390:                 body["max_tokens"] = _hard_cap

 1392:         if response_format:
 1393:             body["response_format"] = response_format
 1394:             # FIX-QWEN-2: Use non-streaming for json_object responses.
 1395:             # Alibaba provider (Qwen 3.5 Plus) returns 502 on json_object+stream.
 1396:             if response_format.get("type") == "json_object" and not reasoning_enabled:
 1397:                 body["stream"] = False
 1398: 
 1399:         # Provider routing from env; empty = let OpenRouter auto-route
 1400:         provider_order_str = os.getenv("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER", "")
 1401:         provider_order = [p.strip() for p in provider_order_str.split(",") if p.strip()]
 1402:         allow_fb = os.getenv("OPENROUTER_ALLOW_FALLBACKS", "true").lower() == "true"

   82: 
   83: Rules:
   84: - ENTAILED: every factual assertion in the SENTENCE is supported by the SPAN. Conservative paraphrase is allowed.
   85: - NEUTRAL: the SENTENCE introduces a fact, entity, mechanism, or specificity NOT present in the SPAN (e.g. SPAN says "GLP-1 RAs", SENTENCE says "semaglutide"; SPAN says "adipocyte metabolism", SENTENCE adds "lipid metabolism" or "energy storage"; SPAN has numbers but not the specific claim being made).
   86: - CONTRADICTED: the SENTENCE asserts something the SPAN explicitly disagrees with.

  100: class _EntailmentJudge:
  101:     """Synchronous httpx wrapper around an OpenRouter entailment call.
  102:

  104:     PG_STRICT_VERIFY_ENTAILMENT=off (the default before I-bug-095).
  105:     """
  106: 
  107:     def __init__(self) -> None:
  108:         import httpx  # local import: avoid forcing the dep when off
  109: 
  110:         # Lazy-import the family-segregation check so the off-mode path
  111:         # never touches openrouter_client. The judge is acting as a
  112:         # content evaluator (Layer-2), so it MUST differ from the
  113:         # generator family per CLAUDE.md §9.1.1 — fail at construction
  114:         # if PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL is in the same family as PG_GENERATOR_MODEL.
  115:         from src.polaris_graph.llm.openrouter_client import check_family_segregation
  116: 
  117:         api_key = os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_API_KEY", "").strip()
  118:         if not api_key:
  119:             raise RuntimeError(
  120:                 "PG_STRICT_VERIFY_ENTAILMENT requires OPENROUTER_API_KEY"
  121:             )
  122:         self._api_key = api_key
  123:         # I-sov-001: endpoint is env-configurable so the sovereign deploy
  124:         # can point the entailment judge at the OVH H200 vLLM endpoint
  125:         # (set OPENROUTER_BASE_URL=http://<priv-ip>:8000/v1). Default keeps

  143:     def judge(self, sentence: str, span: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
  144:         """Return (verdict, reason).
  145: 
  146:         verdict is one of "ENTAILED", "NEUTRAL", "CONTRADICTED".
  147:         On API/parse failure returns ("ENTAILED", "judge_error: ...") —
  148:         fail-open so a transient OpenRouter outage does not nuke a run.
  149: 
  150:         I-bug-100: after each successful httpx call this method records
  151:         the call cost via openrouter_client's module-level helpers
  152:         (`_add_run_cost`, `check_run_budget`, `_COST_LEDGER_PATH`) so
  153:         judge spend is visible to the per-run budget cap and the cost
  154:         ledger. `BudgetExceededError` is explicitly re-raised before
  155:         the broad `except Exception` fail-open handler so a cap breach
  156:         aborts the sweep cleanly instead of being masked as a transient
  157:         judge error.
  158:         """
  159:         prompt = _ENTAILMENT_PROMPT.format(span=span, sentence=sentence)
  160:         started = time.monotonic()
  161:         try:
  162:             response = self._client.post(
  163:                 self._endpoint,
  164:                 headers={
  165:                     "Authorization": f"Bearer {self._api_key}",
  166:                     "Content-Type": "application/json",
  167:                 },
  168:                 json={
  169:                     "model": self._model,
  170:                     "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
  171:                     "temperature": 0.0,
  172:                     "max_tokens": 100,
  173:                     "response_format": {"type": "json_object"},
  174:                 },
  175:             )
  176:             response.raise_for_status()

  178: 
  179:             # I-safety-002b (#925): Path-B gate capture. The entailment judge is the
  180:             # evaluator-family LLM call that bypasses OpenRouterClient (direct httpx),
  181:             # so without capturing here the gate's two-family completeness check would
  182:             # be a silent no-op. Best-effort + gate-flagged; lazy import keeps off-mode
  183:             # import cost zero. `data` is the genuinely-served non-stream JSON.
  184:             try:
  185:                 from src.polaris_graph.benchmark import pathB_capture as _pathb
  186:                 if _pathb.is_active():
  187:                     _pathb.capture_llm_call(
  188:                         role="evaluator",
  189:                         messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
  190:                         raw_response=data,
  191:                     )
  192:             except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — capture must never break the judge
  193:                 pass
  194: 
  195:             # I-bug-100: cost recording. Reads + records BEFORE verdict
  196:             # parse so a cap breach aborts the sweep regardless of
  197:             # downstream parse outcome.
  198:             usage = data.get("usage", {}) or {}
  199:             input_tokens = int(usage.get("prompt_tokens", 0) or 0)
  200:             output_tokens = int(usage.get("completion_tokens", 0) or 0)
  201:             api_cost = float(usage.get("cost", 0) or 0)
  202:             actual_cost = api_cost or _orc._impute_cost_from_tokens(
  203:                 self._model, input_tokens, output_tokens, 0,
  204:             )
  205:             # I-bug-100 iter-1 diff P2 fix: when the entire usage block
  206:             # is absent, both api_cost and the imputed value are 0, which
  207:             # silently bypasses the budget guard. Fall back to a
  208:             # conservative estimate based on typical judge-call shape
  209:             # (~500 prompt + ~100 completion tokens) priced at Opus-tier
  210:             # so the budget cap is preserved on degraded responses.
  211:             if actual_cost == 0 and not usage:
  212:                 actual_cost = _orc._impute_cost_from_tokens(
  213:                     self._model, 500, 100, 0,
  214:                 )
  215:             _orc._add_run_cost(actual_cost)
  216:             duration_ms = (time.monotonic() - started) * 1000.0
  217:             try:
  218:                 _append_judge_ledger_entry(
  219:                     input_tokens=input_tokens,
  220:                     output_tokens=output_tokens,
  221:                     duration_ms=duration_ms,
  222:                     actual_cost=actual_cost,
  223:                 )
  224:             except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — ledger IO is non-critical
  225:                 logger.warning("entailment ledger write failed: %s", exc)
  226:             _orc.check_run_budget(0)  # raises BudgetExceededError if cap breached
  227: 
  228:             content = data["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]
  229:             parsed = json.loads(content)
  230:             verdict = str(parsed.get("verdict", "")).upper().strip()
  231:             reason = str(parsed.get("reason", ""))
  232:             if verdict not in ("ENTAILED", "NEUTRAL", "CONTRADICTED"):
  233:                 return "ENTAILED", f"judge_error: bad_verdict={verdict!r}"
  234:             return verdict, reason
  235:         except _orc.BudgetExceededError:
  236:             # I-bug-100: do NOT fail-open on cap breach. Propagate so
  237:             # the sweep aborts with a clear cause.
  238:             raise
  239:         except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — fail-open by design
  240:             logger.warning("entailment judge error: %s", exc)
  241:             return "ENTAILED", f"judge_error: {type(exc).__name__}"

  244: def _append_judge_ledger_entry(
  245:     *,
  246:     input_tokens: int,
  247:     output_tokens: int,
  248:     duration_ms: float,
  249:     actual_cost: float,
  250: ) -> None:
  251:     """Append a single entailment-judge call to the cost ledger.
  252: 
  253:     Schema mirrors `openrouter_client.OpenRouterClient._append_ledger`
  254:     (line ~481-491) so per-run filters that key on `session_id` /
  255:     `call_type` (e.g., scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py) include judge
  256:     calls without code changes downstream.

    4: `model_pin.json` is non-gating telemetry, `OPENROUTER_ALLOW_FALLBACKS` defaults true, and
    5: "full power" silently degrades if a retrieval key is missing. This gate makes the run

   25: # many *_MAX_TOKENS / *_TOKEN_BUDGET knobs — those are config, not secrets.

   36: # (Codex P1: retrieval creds/knobs were missing from the whole-surface enumeration).

   42: def full_control_surface(roots: list[Path]) -> list[str]:
   43:     """Complete run-affecting env set = enumerated PG_*/OPENROUTER_* UNION the extra
   44:     retrieval/credential env (Codex P1 — these affect the run but aren't prefix-matched)."""
   45:     return sorted(set(enumerate_control_surface(roots)) | set(_EXTRA_CONTROL_ENV))
   46: 
   47: 
   48: def control_surface_sources(roots: list[Path]) -> dict[str, list[str]]:
   49:     """name -> sorted ['<relpath>:<lineno>', ...] provenance for each control var (Codex P2)."""
   50:     extra = "|".join(re.escape(n) for n in _EXTRA_CONTROL_ENV)
   51:     pat = re.compile(
   52:         rf"os\.(?:getenv|environ\.get)\(\s*['\"]((?:PG_|OPENROUTER_)[A-Z0-9_]+|{extra})['\"]"
   53:         rf"|os\.environ\[\s*['\"]((?:PG_|OPENROUTER_)[A-Z0-9_]+|{extra})['\"]"
   54:     )
   55:     out: dict[str, set[str]] = {}
   56:     for root in roots:
   57:         for py in root.rglob("*.py"):
   58:             try:
   59:                 lines = py.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore").splitlines()
   60:             except OSError:
   61:                 continue
   62:             for i, line in enumerate(lines, 1):
   63:                 for m in pat.finditer(line):
   64:                     name = m.group(1) or m.group(2)
   65:                     out.setdefault(name, set()).add(f"{py.as_posix()}:{i}")
   66:     return {k: sorted(v) for k, v in out.items()}

   72: )

   75: class GateError(RuntimeError):
   76:     """Fatal gate violation — the run is INVALID and must be discarded, never scored."""
   77: 
   78: 
   79: def is_secret_var(name: str) -> bool:
   80:     """True iff `name` is a credential whose VALUE must be redacted (not a *_TOKENS knob)."""
   81:     if name in _SECRET_EXPLICIT:
   82:         return True
   83:     if name.endswith(("_MAX_TOKENS", "_TOKENS", "_TOKEN_BUDGET")):
   84:         return False
   85:     return name.endswith(_SECRET_SUFFIXES)
   86: 
   87: 
   88: def enumerate_control_surface(roots: list[Path]) -> list[str]:
   89:     """Scan source for every PG_*/OPENROUTER_* env var actually read (Codex: complete set).
   90: 
   91:     Greps os.getenv / os.environ.get / os.environ[...] reads — NOT a handpicked list.
   92:     """
   93:     pat = re.compile(
   94:         r"os\.(?:getenv|environ\.get)\(\s*['\"]((?:PG_|OPENROUTER_)[A-Z0-9_]+)['\"]"
   95:         r"|os\.environ\[\s*['\"]((?:PG_|OPENROUTER_)[A-Z0-9_]+)['\"]"
   96:     )
   97:     found: set[str] = set()
   98:     for root in roots:
   99:         for py in root.rglob("*.py"):
  100:             try:
  101:                 text = py.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
  102:             except OSError:
  103:                 continue
  104:             for m in pat.finditer(text):
  105:                 found.add(m.group(1) or m.group(2))
  106:     return sorted(found)
  107: 
  108: 
  109: def _redact(name: str, value: str | None, salt: bytes) -> dict:
  110:     """Secret presence record: present/length/salted-HMAC only — never the value (Codex P1)."""
  111:     if value is None:
  112:         return {"present": False, "length": 0, "salted_hmac": None}
  113:     digest = hmac.new(salt, value.encode("utf-8"), hashlib.sha256).hexdigest()
  114:     return {"present": True, "length": len(value), "salted_hmac": digest}
  115: 
  116: 
  117: def build_effective_config(control_vars: list[str], salt: bytes) -> dict:
  118:     """Snapshot the full control surface; secret VALUES redacted (Codex P1)."""
  119:     cfg: dict[str, dict] = {}
  120:     for name in control_vars:
  121:         val = os.environ.get(name)
  122:         if is_secret_var(name):
  123:             cfg[name] = {"secret": True, **_redact(name, val, salt)}
  124:         else:
  125:             cfg[name] = {"secret": False, "value": val, "set": val is not None}
  126:     return cfg
  127: 
  128: 
  129: def effective_config_hash(cfg: dict) -> str:
  130:     return hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(cfg, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
  234: def resolve_canonical_slug(model_slug: str) -> str | None:
  235:     """I-bug-945 (#931): Resolve OpenRouter alias to its dated canonical_slug at preflight.
  236: 
  237:     OpenRouter exposes a list at GET /api/v1/models with `id` (alias) + `canonical_slug`
  238:     (dated snapshot) per entry. The chat-completions response returns `model=<canonical_slug>`
  239:     while the env pin uses `<id>`. Resolving at preflight lets `assert_post_run` accept the
  240:     served canonical_slug without losing pre-registration integrity — the resolved value is
  241:     persisted in `pathB_gate_pin.json` and becomes the audit anchor.
  242: 
  243:     Returns the canonical_slug, or None if it equals model_slug (no dated suffix exposed).
  244:     Raises GateError if the slug is not in the catalog (fail closed) — Codex P2#2.
  245:     """
  246:     import requests
  247:     api_key = os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_API_KEY")
  248:     headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}"} if api_key else {}
  249:     try:
  250:         r = requests.get("https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/models", headers=headers, timeout=20)
  251:         r.raise_for_status()
  252:         data = r.json().get("data", [])
  253:     except Exception as exc:
  254:         raise GateError(f"OpenRouter models catalog unreachable: {exc}") from exc
  255:     for m in data:
  256:         if m.get("id") == model_slug:
  257:             cs = m.get("canonical_slug")
  258:             return cs if cs and cs != model_slug else None
  259:     raise GateError(f"OpenRouter catalog has no entry for pinned slug {model_slug!r} (alias unknown)")
  260: 
  261: 
  262: def real_retrieval_prober(backend: str) -> bool:
  263:     """Minimal live reachability ping per backend (Codex P1). Returns True iff a valid
  264:     response. Cheap; runs once at preflight. Imported lazily to keep the module light."""
  265:     import requests
  266:     try:
  267:         if backend == "serper":
  268:             r = requests.post(
  269:                 "https://google.serper.dev/search",
  270:                 headers={"X-API-KEY": os.environ["SERPER_API_KEY"], "Content-Type": "application/json"},
  271:                 json={"q": "metformin"}, timeout=15,
  272:             )
  273:             return r.status_code == 200
  274:         if backend == "semantic_scholar":
  275:             r = requests.get(
  276:                 "https://api.semanticscholar.org/graph/v1/paper/search",
  277:                 headers={"x-api-key": os.environ["SEMANTIC_SCHOLAR_API_KEY"]},
  278:                 params={"query": "metformin", "limit": 1}, timeout=20,
  279:             )
  280:             return r.status_code == 200
  281:     except Exception:
  282:         return False
  283:     return False

  295: def assert_post_run(
  296:     pin: dict,
  297:     control_vars: list[str],
  298:     salt: bytes,
  299:     calls: list[LLMCall],
  300:     retrieval_backends_attempted: set[str],
  301: ) -> dict:
  302:     """Fatal post-run gate (Codex). Any violation ⇒ run INVALID, discard + re-run.
  303: 
  304:     Returns the established per-role served-identity surrogates on success."""
  305:     # config no-drift — rebuild from the SAME resolved surface preflight pinned (not a
  306:     # caller-passed list, which could differ / bypass; Codex iter-2).
  307:     pinned_vars = pin.get("control_vars", control_vars)
  308:     cfg_now = effective_config_hash(build_effective_config(pinned_vars, salt))
  309:     if cfg_now != pin["effective_config_hash"]:
  310:         raise GateError("effective_config drifted between preflight and post-run")
  311:     pins_by_role = {rp["role"]: rp for rp in pin["role_pins"]}
  312:     if not calls:
  313:         raise GateError("no LLM calls captured — completeness check cannot pass")
  314:     # COMPLETENESS: every pinned role must appear (Codex P1 — uncaptured evaluator/judge invisible)
  315:     roles_seen = {c.role for c in calls}
  316:     missing_roles = set(pins_by_role) - roles_seen
  317:     if missing_roles:
  318:         raise GateError(f"completeness: pinned role(s) with no captured LLM call: {missing_roles}")
  319:     surrogate_by_role: dict[str, set[str]] = {}
  320:     for c in calls:
  321:         if not (c.prompt_messages_present and c.request_hash and c.response_metadata):
  322:             raise GateError(f"call {c.call_id}: incomplete capture (prompt/request_hash/metadata)")
  323:         rp = pins_by_role.get(c.role)
  324:         if rp is None:
  325:             raise GateError(f"call {c.call_id}: role {c.role!r} not pinned")
  326:         for fld in rp["surrogate_fields"]:
  327:             if fld not in c.response_metadata:
  328:                 raise GateError(f"call {c.call_id}: served metadata missing surrogate field {fld!r}")
  329:         # EXACT provider + EXACT full-slug model match (Codex P1 — no loose substring).
  330:         # I-bug-944 (#925 smoke #13): provider comparison is case-insensitive (OpenRouter
  331:         # returns "Fireworks" / "DeepInfra" with title case while the pin env var
  332:         # OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER is documented lower-case; case-mismatch is identity-
  333:         # equivalent and must not gate-fail an otherwise full-power run). Model slug stays
  334:         # case-sensitive — slugs are canonical.
  335:         served_provider = (c.response_metadata.get("provider_name") or "").strip().lower()
  336:         pinned_provider = (rp["provider_name"] or "").strip().lower()
  337:         if served_provider != pinned_provider:
  338:             raise GateError(f"call {c.call_id}: served provider {c.response_metadata.get('provider_name')!r} != pinned {rp['provider_name']!r}")
  339:         # I-bug-945 (#931): accept served model matching EITHER the pinned alias OR the
  340:         # canonical_slug resolved at preflight. The OpenRouter chat-completions response
  341:         # returns `model=<canonical_slug>` while the env pin is the alias; both are identity-
  342:         # equivalent and recorded in the persisted pin (pathB_gate_pin.json).
  343:         served_model = c.response_metadata.get("model")
  344:         accepted_models = {rp["model_slug"]}
  345:         if rp.get("canonical_slug"):
  346:             accepted_models.add(rp["canonical_slug"])
  347:         if served_model not in accepted_models:
  348:             raise GateError(
  349:                 f"call {c.call_id}: served model {served_model!r} matches neither pinned "
  350:                 f"alias {rp['model_slug']!r} nor canonical_slug {rp.get('canonical_slug')!r}"
  351:             )
  352:         # I-bug-945 P2#4 (Codex): normalize served `model` to the alias before surrogate
  353:         # compute, so a same-role mix of alias and canonical_slug calls produces a single
  354:         # surrogate value (otherwise raw-model drift would false-fail the mid-run check).
  355:         normalized_metadata = dict(c.response_metadata)
  356:         normalized_metadata["model"] = rp["model_slug"]
  357:         surrogate_by_role.setdefault(c.role, set()).add(_role_surrogate(normalized_metadata, rp["surrogate_fields"]))
  358:     # per-role served identity must be SINGLE-VALUED across the run (no mid-run drift, Codex P1)
  359:     for role, ids in surrogate_by_role.items():
  360:         if len(ids) != 1:
  361:             raise GateError(f"role {role}: served-identity surrogate drifted across calls ({len(ids)} distinct)")
  362:     # required retrieval backends were ACTUALLY attempted (Codex iter-5 P2)
  363:     required = set(_REQUIRED_RETRIEVAL_CREDS_TO_BACKENDS.values())
  364:     not_attempted = required - retrieval_backends_attempted
  365:     if not_attempted:
  366:         raise GateError(f"required retrieval backends never attempted this run: {not_attempted}")
  367:     return {"served_identity_by_role": {r: next(iter(ids)) for r, ids in surrogate_by_role.items()}}
  368:

  371:     "SERPER_API_KEY": "serper",
  372:     "SEMANTIC_SCHOLAR_API_KEY": "semantic_scholar",
  373: }

    2: 
    3: Per-sentence check enforcing:
    4:   (a) at least one provenance token present
    5:   (b) every token references an evidence_id in the pool
    6:   (c) span bounds are valid (0 <= start <= end <= len(text))
    7:   (d) every decimal in the sentence appears in the cited spans
    8:   (e) sentence and span share >= MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP content words
    9:   (f) I-bug-092: span semantically ENTAILS the sentence's specific claims
   10:       (gated behind PG_STRICT_VERIFY_ENTAILMENT, defaults off)
   11: 
   12: Checks (a)-(e) are mechanical "provenance hygiene" — they bound a claim to
   13: the same TOPIC as its span. Check (f) is "provenance correctness" — it
   14: verifies the span actually entails the sentence's specific facts. The
   15: audit on 2026-05-09 found that a capable generator can pass (a)-(e) by
   16: producing topically-overlapping prose that introduces unsourced specifics
   17: (e.g. inserting "pancreatic β-cells", "lipid metabolism", "energy storage"
   18: into a span that says only "synergistic actions on insulin secretion,
   19: glucagon suppression, appetite regulation, and adipocyte metabolism").

   22: constructs a VerifiedSentence for use by the generator orchestrator.

   25:   PG_PROVENANCE_MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP — minimum shared content words (default 2)

   70: 
   71: # Minimal English stopword list. Strict-verify's content-word overlap should
   72: # count substantive vocabulary, not function words. This is intentionally
   73: # small — the rule is conservative ("at least 2 shared content words")
   74: # so even a short stoplist yields the right behavior.
   75: _STOPWORDS: frozenset[str] = frozenset({
   76:     "a", "an", "the", "and", "or", "but", "if", "of", "in", "on", "at",
   77:     "to", "for", "with", "as", "by", "from", "into", "through", "during",

   83:     "your", "i", "me", "my", "he", "she", "his", "her",
   84: })
   85:

   88:

   90: def _min_overlap_threshold() -> int:
   91:     raw = os.environ.get("PG_PROVENANCE_MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP", "")
   92:     try:
   93:         return max(0, int(raw))
   94:     except ValueError:
   95:         return DEFAULT_MIN_CONTENT_OVERLAP
   96: 
   97: 
   98: def _content_words(text: str) -> set[str]:
   99:     """Lowercase content words (>=3 chars, not stopwords) from `text`."""
  100:     return {

  103:         if len(m.group(0)) >= 3 and m.group(0).lower() not in _STOPWORDS

    1: """Tests for I-bug-100 — entailment-judge cost recording.
    2: 
    3: After every successful entailment judge call, the cost is recorded:
    4: 1. `_add_run_cost(cost_usd)` increments the per-run accumulator.
    5: 2. An entry is appended to `pg_cost_ledger.jsonl` matching the
    6:    OpenRouterClient schema (`session_id` / `call_type` /
    7:    `input_tokens` / `output_tokens` / `reasoning_tokens` /
    8:    `duration_ms` / `cost_usd` / `cumulative_cost_usd`).
    9: 3. `check_run_budget(0)` raises `BudgetExceededError` if the call
   10:    pushed cumulative cost past `PG_MAX_COST_PER_RUN`.
   11: 
   12: `BudgetExceededError` MUST escape the fail-open broad-except handler
   13: so a cap breach aborts the sweep instead of being masked as a
   14: transient judge error.
   15: 
   16: Test isolation pattern:
   17: - Patch `openrouter_client._COST_LEDGER_PATH` to a tmp file via
   18:   `monkeypatch.setattr` (NOT setenv: the path is bound at import).
   19: - Patch `openrouter_client.PG_MAX_COST_PER_RUN` similarly for the
   20:   cap-breach test.
   21: - Reset `_RUN_COST_CTX` per test via `reset_run_cost()`.
   22: - entailment_judge accesses these via `_orc.<attr>` so monkeypatch

   72: def test_judge_records_api_cost_when_present(monkeypatch, tmp_path):
   73:     """When OpenRouter response includes `usage.cost`, that value is
   74:     recorded verbatim (not imputed) in both the run-cost accumulator

   95: 
   96:     # Run-cost accumulator picked up the API-reported cost
   97:     assert openrouter_client.current_run_cost() == pytest.approx(0.001234)

  100:     lines = ledger_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").strip().splitlines()

  108:     assert "session_id" in entry
